## Data fix for NonAuthCapture Transactions (PR:2660)
UPDATE transactions
    JOIN payments
    ON transactions.entity_id = payments.id
    SET transactions.fee = 0,
        transactions.service_tax = 0
    WHERE payments.captured_at is null AND
          transactions.fee > 0;

DELETE FROM fees_breakup
    WHERE transaction_id IN (
        SELECT transactions.id
            FROM transactions
            JOIN payments
            ON transactions.entity_id = payments.id
            WHERE payments.captured_at is null AND
                  transactions.fee > 0
        );

UPDATE settlements
SET attempts = (
    SELECT COUNT(id) FROM fund_transfer_attempts
    WHERE fund_transfer_attempts.source_id = settlements.id
    AND fund_transfer_attempts.source_type = 'settlement'
    GROUP BY fund_transfer_attempts.source_id
);

UPDATE settlements s1 JOIN
(
    SELECT t1.id, t1.source_id, t1.remarks
    FROM fund_transfer_attempts AS t1 JOIN
    (
        SELECT MAX(created_at) as latest, source_id
        FROM fund_transfer_attempts
        GROUP BY source_id
    ) AS t2
    ON t1.source_id = t2.source_id AND t1.created_at = t2.latest
) AS t3
ON s1.id = t3.source_id
SET s1.remarks = t3.remarks
WHERE t3.remarks IS NOT NULL
AND s1.remarks IS NULL;

update daily_settlements join
(
    select batch_fund_transfer_id, count(*) as processed_count
    from settlements
    where status = 'processed'
    group by batch_fund_transfer_id
) as stats
on daily_settlements.id =  stats.`batch_fund_transfer_id`
set daily_settlements.processed_count = stats.processed_count;

update daily_settlements join
(
    select batch_fund_transfer_id, count(*) as processed_count
    from fund_transfer_attempts
    where status = 'processed'
    group by batch_fund_transfer_id
) as stats
on daily_settlements.id =  stats.`batch_fund_transfer_id`
set daily_settlements.processed_count = stats.processed_count;

update daily_settlements join
(
    select batch_fund_transfer_id, sum(amount) as processed_amount
    from settlements
    group by batch_fund_transfer_id
) as stats
on daily_settlements.id =  stats.`batch_fund_transfer_id`
set daily_settlements.processed_amount = stats.processed_amount;

update daily_settlements join
(
    select fund_transfer_attempts.batch_fund_transfer_id, sum(settlements.amount) as processed_amount
    from fund_transfer_attempts join settlements
    on fund_transfer_attempts.source_id = settlements.`id`
    where fund_transfer_attempts.status = 'processed'
    and fund_transfer_attempts.batch_fund_transfer_id = settlements.batch_fund_transfer_id
    group by fund_transfer_attempts.batch_fund_transfer_id
) as stats
on daily_settlements.id =  stats.`batch_fund_transfer_id`
set daily_settlements.processed_amount = stats.processed_amount;

update settlements set attempts=1 where id = '7O0p1u35YddfsU';

# Update batch id for settlements created via attempt flow
Update settlements
JOIN
  (SELECT source_id,
          max(fund_transfer_attempts.batch_fund_transfer_id) AS batch_id
   FROM fund_transfer_attempts
   JOIN settlements ON settlements.id = fund_transfer_attempts.source_id
   GROUP BY source_id) AS t ON t.source_id = settlements.id
SET settlements.batch_fund_transfer_id = t.batch_id
WHERE settlements.batch_fund_transfer_id IS NULL;

update daily_settlements join
(
    select batch_fund_transfer_id, count(*) as processed_count, sum(amount) as processed_amount
    from settlements
    where status = 'processed'
    group by batch_fund_transfer_id
) as stats
on daily_settlements.id =  stats.`batch_fund_transfer_id`
set daily_settlements.processed_count = stats.processed_count,
daily_settlements.processed_amount = stats.processed_amount;

# Post deployment of #3125

# For all old entries (gross_amount would be null), set tax_amount to 0 and gross_amount = amount.
UPDATE invoices SET
    tax_amount = 0,
    gross_amount = amount
WHERE gross_amount IS NULL AND amount IS NOT NULL;

# For all old entries (gross_amount would be null), set gross_amount, tax_amount and net_amount.
UPDATE line_items SET
    gross_amount = amount * quantity,
    tax_amount = 0,
    net_amount = gross_amount
WHERE gross_amount IS NULL;

    SET type=1
    WHERE gateway in (

    );

    SET type=2
    WHERE
        card=0
        AND gateway NOT IN (
                'sharp', 'atom', 'wallet_openwallet'
            );

# Updates merchant_id in fund_transfer_attempts
update fund_transfer_attempts f join
(
    select id, merchant_id
    from settlements
) as s
on f.source_id = s.id
set f.merchant_id = s.merchant_id;

# Post deployment of branch order-partial-payments

# Updates amount_paid value for old rows
UPDATE orders SET amount_paid = amount where status = 'paid' and amount_paid = 0;

# Update settled_on, processed_at in settlement table
update settlements s
join
(
SELECT source_id, UNIX_TIMESTAMP(STR_TO_DATE(date_time, '%d/%m/%Y %H:%i:%s')) AS processed_at_timestamp, (UNIX_TIMESTAMP(DATE(STR_TO_DATE(date_time, '%d/%m/%Y %H:%i:%s')))) AS settled_at_timestamp
FROM fund_transfer_attempts
WHERE fund_transfer_attempts.status = 'processed'
AND fund_transfer_attempts.`date_time` is not null
) f
ON s.id = f.source_id
SET s.processed_at = f.processed_at_timestamp,
s.settled_on = f.settled_at_timestamp;

# Update settled_on, processed_at in payout table
update payouts
set processed_at = updated_at, settled_on = updated_at
where utr is not null
and processed_at is null;

######## Queries run for merchant invoices
UPDATE merchant_invoice
JOIN
  (SELECT merchant_id,
          amount
   FROM adjustment
   WHERE description = 'GST reversal') AS t ON merchant_invoice.merchant_id = t.merchant_id
SET tax = t.amount
WHERE MONTH = 7
  AND YEAR = 2017
  AND TYPE = 'card_lte_2k';

# Adding the settlement id in the transfers table
UPDATE transfers as tr
    JOIN payments as p
        ON p.transfer_id = tr.id
    JOIN transactions as txn
        ON txn.entity_id = p.id
    SET recipient_settlement_id = txn.settlement_id
    WHERE txn.type = 'payment'
    AND p.transfer_id IS NOT NULL

UPDATE merchant_invoice
JOIN merchant_details ON merchant_details.merchant_id = merchant_invoice.merchant_id
SET merchant_invoice.gstin = merchant_details.gstin
WHERE (merchant_invoice.gstin IS NULL or merchant_invoice.gstin = '')
    AND merchant_details.gstin IS NOT NULL
    AND merchant_details.gstin != '';

UPDATE merchant_invoice
JOIN merchant_details ON merchant_details.merchant_id = merchant_invoice.merchant_id
SET merchant_invoice.gstin = merchant_details.p_gstin
WHERE (merchant_invoice.gstin IS NULL OR merchant_invoice.gstin = '')
    AND merchant_details.p_gstin IS NOT NULL
    AND merchant_details.p_gstin != '';

UPDATE payments
    JOIN hdfc ON hdfc.payment_id = payments.id
    SET payments.reference2 = hdfc.auth
WHERE hdfc.action = 4 AND
    hdfc.status = "authorized" AND
    hdfc.auth IS NOT NULL AND
    payments.gateway = "hdfc" AND
    payments.reference2 is NULL;

UPDATE payments
    JOIN first_data ON first_data.payment_id = payments.id
    SET payments.reference2 = first_data.auth_code
WHERE first_data.action = "capture" AND
    first_data.status = "CAPTURED" AND
    first_data.transaction_result = "APPROVED" AND
    first_data.auth_code IS NOT NULL AND
    payments.gateway = "first_data" AND
    (payments.reference2 is NULL OR payments.reference2 = "00");

UPDATE payments
    JOIN axis ON axis.payment_id = payments.id
    SET payments.reference2 = axis.vpc_AuthorizeId
WHERE axis.action = "authorize" AND
    axis.vpc_TxnResponseCode = "0" AND
    axis.received = 1 AND
    axis.vpc_AuthorizeId IS NOT NULL AND
    payments.gateway = "axis_migs" AND
    payments.reference2 is NULL;

UPDATE payments
    JOIN cybersource ON cybersource.payment_id = payments.id
    SET payments.reference2 = cybersource.authorizationCode
WHERE cybersource.action = "authorize" AND
    cybersource.status = "authorized" AND
    cybersource.received = 1 AND
    cybersource.authorizationCode IS NOT NULL AND
    payments.gateway = "cybersource" AND
    payments.reference2 is NULL;

UPDATE payments
    SET reference1 = null
WHERE method = "card";

# PR:5366 Extracting auth code from approval code
UPDATE `first_data`
    SET `auth_code` = SUBSTR(`approval_code`,3,6)
WHERE
    `action` IN ('authorize', 'purchase') AND
    `approval_code` LIKE 'Y:%';

    JOIN first_data ON first_data.payment_id = payments.id
    SET payments.reference2 = first_data.auth_code
WHERE
    first_data.action IN ('authorize', 'purchase') AND
    (first_data.auth_code IS NOT NULL AND first_data.auth_code != '00') AND
    payments.gateway = "first_data" AND
    (payments.reference2 is NULL OR payments.reference2 = "00") AND
    payments.status != 'failed';

# BEFORE #5703 IS DEPLOYED
#
# UPDATE
#   terminals t2 INNER JOIN terminals t1
#   ON
#     t1.merchant_id=t2.merchant_id AND
#     (t1.type=3 OR t1.type=2) AND
#     t2.type=4 AND
#     t1.gateway=t2.gateway AND
#     t1.gateway='first_data'
#   SET t2.gateway_merchant_id2=t1.gateway_merchant_id;
#
# ^This is the query that is to be run, but since only 7 terminals are
# going to be affected, we selected first, then updated individually.

UPDATE terminals SET gateway_merchant_id2='3300225673'
    WHERE gateway_merchant_id='3300204071' AND type=4 AND deleted_at = NULL;
UPDATE terminals SET gateway_merchant_id2='3300230288'
    WHERE gateway_merchant_id='3300230378' AND type=4 AND deleted_at = NULL;
UPDATE terminals SET gateway_merchant_id2='3300230223'
    WHERE gateway_merchant_id='3300230224' AND type=4 AND deleted_at = NULL;
UPDATE terminals SET gateway_merchant_id2='3300230668'
    WHERE gateway_merchant_id='3300230669' AND type=4 AND deleted_at = NULL;
UPDATE terminals SET gateway_merchant_id2='3387000778'
    WHERE gateway_merchant_id='3387000801' AND type=4 AND deleted_at = NULL;
UPDATE terminals SET gateway_merchant_id2='3300231186'
    WHERE gateway_merchant_id='3300231185' AND type=4 AND deleted_at = NULL;
UPDATE terminals SET gateway_merchant_id2='3387001866'
    WHERE gateway_merchant_id='3387001867' AND type=4 AND deleted_at = NULL;

# AFTER #5703 IS DEPLOYED
UPDATE
  terminals
  SET gateway_merchant_id2 = NULL
  WHERE
    gateway='first_data' AND
    gateway_merchant_id IN (
        '3374679283',
        '3374679291',
        '3374679309',
        '3374679333',
        '3396093976');

UPDATE transactions SET settled_at=1509942600 WHERE id='8wulvPuP2Xu7Mj';

# Fix user email case.
UPDATE users AS u SET u.email = Lower(u.email) WHERE u.email != Lower(u.email) LIMIT 100;

# Corrects Bank Transfer IMPS Bank Codes used in bank accounts
UPDATE bank_accounts INNER JOIN bank_transfers
  ON bank_accounts.id=bank_transfers.payer_bank_account_id
  SET bank_accounts.ifsc_code = 'UTBI0XCNA10'
  WHERE bank_transfers.mode='imps' and bank_transfers.payer_ifsc like 'UBI%';

UPDATE bank_accounts INNER JOIN bank_transfers
  ON bank_accounts.id=bank_transfers.payer_bank_account_id
  SET bank_accounts.ifsc_code = 'UBIN0538167'
  WHERE bank_transfers.mode='imps' and bank_transfers.payer_ifsc like 'UOB%';

# We were told by Kotak that H2H won't work on 2nd Dec between 3pm and 10pm.
# So, settling all the transactions which were supposed to be settled during this
# time, at 2pm itself. More details in the PR #6371
UPDATE transactions
SET settled_at = 1512203400
WHERE created_at < 1512201600
  AND settled_at >= 1512207000
  AND settled_at < 1512214200
  AND on_hold = 0
  AND settled = 0
  AND (TYPE = 'payment'
       OR TYPE = 'refund') LIMIT 5906

# UTIB0000001 is not a valid IFSC, but we were still receiving it for
# RTGS payments from Axis. Those are now being replaced with a different
# Axis IFSC, and this queries updates the older payer bank accounts.
UPDATE bank_accounts INNER JOIN bank_transfers
  ON bank_accounts.id=bank_transfers.payer_bank_account_id
  SET bank_accounts.ifsc_code = 'UTIB0001918'
  WHERE bank_transfers.mode='rtgs' and bank_accounts.ifsc_code='UTIB0000001';

# Update activation status
UPDATE `merchant_details` INNER JOIN `merchants`
ON `merchant_details`.`merchant_id` = `merchants`.`id`
SET `merchant_details`.`activation_status` = 'activated'
WHERE `merchant_details`.`submitted_at` IS NOT NULL AND `merchants`.`activated_at` IS NOT NULL AND `merchants`.`archived_at` IS NULL;

UPDATE `merchant_details` INNER JOIN `merchants`
ON `merchant_details`.`merchant_id` = `merchants`.`id`
SET `merchant_details`.`activation_status` = 'under_review'
WHERE `merchant_details`.`submitted_at` IS NOT NULL AND `merchants`.`activated_at` IS NULL AND `merchants`.`archived_at` IS NULL;

UPDATE `merchant_details` INNER JOIN `merchants`
ON `merchant_details`.`merchant_id` = `merchants`.`id`
SET `merchant_details`.`activation_status` = 'needs_clarification', `merchant_details`.`clarification_mode` = 'email'
WHERE `merchant_details`.`submitted_at` IS NOT NULL AND `merchants`.`activated_at` IS NULL AND `merchants`.`archived_at` IS NOT NULL;

UPDATE `merchant_details` INNER JOIN `merchants`
ON `merchant_details`.`merchant_id` = `merchants`.`id`
SET `merchant_details`.`archived_at` = `merchants`.`archived_at`;

update settlements join fund_transfer_attempts
on settlements.id = fund_transfer_attempts.source_id
set settlements.utr = fund_transfer_attempts.utr
where settlements.channel = 'icici'
and settlements.`batch_fund_transfer_id` = fund_transfer_attempts.`batch_fund_transfer_id`
and settlements.utr is null
and fund_transfer_attempts.utr is not null;

update emi_plans set deleted_at = now() where subvention = 'merchant';

update emi_plans set merchant_payback = ROUND(10000 * (duration * rate/120000 * POWER(1 + rate/120000 , duration) - POWER(1 + rate/120000, duration) + 1)/ (duration * rate/120000 * POWER(1 + rate/120000, duration)));

// setting it to max int (jan 19 2038)
// between nov 1st 2017 and feb 5th 2018
UPDATE tokens SET expired_at = 2147483647 WHERE method='netbanking' AND recurring_status IS NOT NULL AND created_at > 1506796200 AND created_at <= 1517853630;

// after feb 5th 2018, 23:30
UPDATE tokens SET expired_at = (UNIX_TIMESTAMP((DATE_ADD(FROM_UNIXTIME(created_at), INTERVAL 10 YEAR)))) WHERE method='netbanking' AND recurring_status IS NOT NULL AND created_at > 1517853630;

update merchant_invoice join merchant_details
on merchant_invoice.merchant_id = merchant_details.merchant_id
set merchant_invoice.gstin = merchant_details.p_gstin
where merchant_invoice.gstin = ''
and merchant_details.gstin = ''
and merchant_details.p_gstin != ''
and merchant_details.p_gstin is not null
and merchant_invoice.year = 2017
and merchant_invoice.month = 12;

update merchant_invoice join merchant_details
on merchant_invoice.merchant_id = merchant_details.merchant_id
set merchant_invoice.gstin = merchant_details.p_gstin
where merchant_invoice.gstin = ''
and merchant_details.gstin = ''
and merchant_details.p_gstin != ''
and merchant_details.p_gstin is not null
and merchant_invoice.year = 2018
and merchant_invoice.month = 1;

WHERE method = 'netbanking';

SET method = 'emandate'
WHERE created_at > 1504243800
  AND terminal_id IN ('91LaFcjGVPBmcu',
                      '8n8nyWExX8l4Oy',
                      '8qH2tMbx3MCP7n',
                      '8yswNFkuG98eN4',
                      '9HxXL7xNhF3KyH',
                      '9QYaAkoHaXO8Hk',
                      '9TNVhZGrDKIQ1R',
                      '9TNbtq22gvZql3',
                      '9Yrjx0YHzWBlVQ',
                      '9YrlbhQML8cd4Y')

-- move emandate payments to auth_type = netbanking:
UPDATE payments
SET auth_type = 'netbanking'
WHERE created_at > 1504243800
  AND recurring_type = 'initial'
  AND method = 'emandate'
  AND terminal_id IN ('91LaFcjGVPBmcu',
                      '8n8nyWExX8l4Oy',
                      '8qH2tMbx3MCP7n',
                      '8yswNFkuG98eN4',
                      '9HxXL7xNhF3KyH',
                      '9QYaAkoHaXO8Hk',
                      '9TNVhZGrDKIQ1R',
                      '9TNbtq22gvZql3',
                      '9Yrjx0YHzWBlVQ',
                      '9YrlbhQML8cd4Y')

-- move orders to emandate method:
UPDATE orders
SET method = 'emandate'
WHERE id IN
    ( SELECT order_id
      FROM payments
      WHERE created_at > 1504243800
        AND terminal_id IN ('91LaFcjGVPBmcu',
                           '8n8nyWExX8l4Oy',
                           '8qH2tMbx3MCP7n',
                           '8yswNFkuG98eN4',
                           '9HxXL7xNhF3KyH',
                           '9QYaAkoHaXO8Hk',
                           '9TNVhZGrDKIQ1R',
                           '9TNbtq22gvZql3',
                           '9Yrjx0YHzWBlVQ',
                           '9YrlbhQML8cd4Y'))

-- move terminals to emandate method:

SET emandate = 1,
netbanking = 0
WHERE id IN ('91LaFcjGVPBmcu',
             '8n8nyWExX8l4Oy',

             '9YrlbhQML8cd4Y')

WHERE m.`parent_id` IS NULL AND md.`submitted_at` IS NOT NULL;

# Update recipient_settlement_id in transfers table
UPDATE transfers as tr
    JOIN payments
        ON payments.transfer_id = tr.id
    JOIN transactions as txn
        ON txn.entity_id = payments.id
    JOIN settlements
        ON txn.settlement_id = settlements.id
SET tr.recipient_settlement_id = settlements.id
WHERE payments.transfer_id IS NOT NULL
AND txn.settled = 1
AND txn.type='payment'
AND tr.recipient_settlement_id IS NULL

# Copies items.tax_rate to line_items.tax_rate for existing entities. Now line_items has tax_rate too.
UPDATE line_items l
       LEFT JOIN items i
              ON l.item_id = i.id
SET    l.tax_rate = i.tax_rate
WHERE  l.tax_rate IS NULL
       AND i.tax_rate IS NOT NULL;

  AND `type` = 'push';

# Udaan data corrections, necessitated by duplicate virtual bank account numbers
# 1. Close the undesired VA, and move the bank_transfers to the desired one
UPDATE
  virtual_accounts INNER JOIN bank_transfers
  ON
    virtual_accounts.id=bank_transfers.virtual_account_id
  SET
    bank_transfers.virtual_account_id='A8xTrQAiKHV3BO',
    virtual_accounts.amount_paid=0,
    virtual_accounts.amount_received=0,
    virtual_accounts.status='closed'
  WHERE bank_transfers.virtual_account_id='A8xTrPsTWeNBzx';
# 2. Update amount fields in the desired VA
UPDATE
  virtual_accounts
  SET
    amount_paid=621400,
    amount_received=621400
  WHERE id='A8xTrQAiKHV3BO';

# Updates created_at for merchant_requests and action_state
UPDATE action_state
  JOIN merchant_requests ON merchant_requests.id = action_state.entity_id
  JOIN (
    SELECT MIN(action_state.created_at) as created_at, action_state.entity_id as merchant_request_id
    FROM action_state
    WHERE action_state.name = "under_review" AND entity_type = "merchant_request"
    GROUP BY action_state.entity_id
  ) as ac_min ON (
    ac_min.created_at = action_state.created_at
    AND ac_min.merchant_request_id = action_state.entity_id
    AND action_state.entity_type = "merchant_request"
    AND action_state.name = "under_review")
  JOIN (
    SELECT SUBSTRING_INDEX(`key`, ".", 1) AS product, entity_id as merchant_id, MIN(created_at) as created_at
    FROM settings
    WHERE module = 'onboarding'
    GROUP BY product, entity_id
  ) as products ON (merchant_requests.merchant_id = products.merchant_id AND merchant_requests.name = products.product)
  SET
      merchant_requests.created_at = products.created_at,
      action_state.created_at = products.created_at
  WHERE merchant_requests.type = "product"

# Updates values for old batches.processed_count
UPDATE batches
    SET processed_count = success_count + failure_count
    WHERE processed_count IS NULL AND processing = 0;

# Updates settings for payment_link's type batches for specific duration (Ref: https://razorpay.atlassian.net/browse/IN-126)
UPDATE settings
SET    value = "0"
WHERE  entity_id IN (SELECT id
                     FROM   batches
                     WHERE  created_at > 1528914600
                            AND created_at < 1530901800
                            AND type = 'payment_link')
LIMIT 120;

# Following is query to mark around 41k links cancelled. This is off case need, a merchant had created these via
# batch(non-api user) and wants them to be cancelled. He didn't input expiration during batch creation.
# Rows matched: 41660  Changed: 41660  Warnings: 0
UPDATE invoices i
LEFT JOIN payments p ON i.id = p.invoice_id
SET i.status = 'cancelled',
    i.cancelled_at = unix_timestamp(),
    i.updated_at = unix_timestamp()
WHERE i.batch_id IN ('AYhD3yazCd4XsG',
                     'AYgupgpbRuvOHj',
                     'AYdhPjiVrXcx01',
                     'AYcljvhrnBiZFN',
                     'AYcWsLPctWyFkF',
                     'AXs966a4fD6xlY',
                     'AXqaVCaHw4sPvS',
                     'AXq88Mrf0yBzSO',
                     'AXpyCGVixrGmis',
                     'AWIQlxCEmkmTBS',
                     'AWINqUuC6npUD3',
                     'AWIKH6eWfdds7u',
                     'AWIC0NbL4uF4Q6',
                     'AWHMpEJsWIMGCu',
                     'AWEak5fOxzrzqt')
  AND i.merchant_id = '9mOxXWuS2uIw5j'
  AND i.status = 'issued'
  AND p.id IS NULL
# Rows matched: 189  Changed: 189  Warnings: 0
UPDATE invoices i
LEFT JOIN payments p ON i.id = p.invoice_id
SET i.status = 'cancelled',
    i.cancelled_at = unix_timestamp(),
    i.updated_at = unix_timestamp()
WHERE i.batch_id IN ('AYhD3yazCd4XsG',
                     'AYgupgpbRuvOHj',
                     'AYdhPjiVrXcx01',
                     'AYcljvhrnBiZFN',
                     'AYcWsLPctWyFkF',
                     'AXs966a4fD6xlY',
                     'AXqaVCaHw4sPvS',
                     'AXq88Mrf0yBzSO',
                     'AXpyCGVixrGmis',
                     'AWIQlxCEmkmTBS',
                     'AWINqUuC6npUD3',
                     'AWIKH6eWfdds7u',
                     'AWIC0NbL4uF4Q6',
                     'AWHMpEJsWIMGCu',
                     'AWEak5fOxzrzqt')
  AND i.merchant_id = '9mOxXWuS2uIw5j'
  AND i.status = 'issued'
  AND p.status = 'failed'

# Fixes Billdesk gateway entities not having RefundId due to timeout
UPDATE billdesk SET RefundId = 'NSCB66303666851' WHERE id = 6739873;

# Updates the global_customer attribute for existing subscriptions
UPDATE subscriptions
SET global_customer = 0
WHERE subscriptions.id IN
    (SELECT id
     FROM subscriptions
     INNER JOIN customers ON subscriptions.customer_id = customers.id
     WHERE customers.global_customer_id IS NULL);

# Populating customer_email
UPDATE subscriptions
INNER JOIN customers ON customers.id=subscriptions.customer_id
SET customer_email=customers.email
WHERE customers.email IS NOT NULL
  AND customer_email IS NOT NULL;

    DROP INDEX nodal_beneficiaries_beneficiary_code_unique,
    ADD UNIQUE INDEX  nodal_beneficiaries_beneficiary_code_channel_unique(beneficiary_code, channel);

#Settled at value changes in refund for report fixes
UPDATE transactions set settled_at = created_at WHERE  type='refund' and settled_at=1

#Sync amex column in merchant_banks with the new card_networks column
UPDATE merchant_banks SET card_networks=127 WHERE amex=1;

# Fixes merchant's entities state introduced because of an issue which is fixed separately.
UPDATE bank_accounts SET deleted_at = NULL WHERE id = 'BikuFg4LjWPaRc' LIMIT 1;
UPDATE virtual_accounts SET status = 'active' WHERE id = 'BikuFWAIzbn1Hb' LIMIT 1;

# Missed to update updated_at in above queries ^
# The virtual account has already received new payments and updated_at is touched.
UPDATE bank_accounts SET updated_at = UNIX_TIMESTAMP() WHERE id = 'BikuFg4LjWPaRc' LIMIT 1;

# Populating type data in schedule table from schedule_task
UPDATE schedules as s INNER JOIN schedule_tasks as st ON s.id = st.schedule_id SET s.type = st.type;

// For Source_id(FeU0MYgas7Rc5D) marking fta as initiated since finops unable to do "update from source" dashboard action
// For Source_id(Ff8ivanGHJ5Jk5) required to be in reversed, updating to initiated, then dashboard action will be used.
UPDATE fund_transfer_attempts
    SET status = "initiated",
    remarks = "manual db update for data-correction",
    updated_at = UNIX_TIMESTAMP(NOW())
    WHERE source_id IN ("FeU0MYgas7Rc5D", "Ff8ivanGHJ5Jk5");

// related to the above data correction query.
// finops tried manual data correction before fts data correction was done.
// transfer webhook was fired and it changed the FTA to the state it was before. updating it back again.
UPDATE fund_transfer_attempts
    SET status = "initiated",
    remarks = "manual db update for data-correction",
    updated_at = UNIX_TIMESTAMP(NOW())
    WHERE id="Ff8ivefzUOVRyK";

// Modifying qr_code table as per new apis
ALTER TABLE qr_code
    ADD name varchar(255),
    ADD usage_type varchar(14),
    ADD customer_id varchar(14),
    ADD status varchar(6),
    ADD description text,
    ADD payments_amount_received bigint default 0,
    ADD payments_received_count int default 0,
    ADD fixed_amount tinyint default 0,
    ADD notes json,
    ADD close_reason varchar(10),
    ADD closed_at int,
    ADD close_by int;

ALTER TABLE qr_code MODIFY entity_id varchar(14) DEFAULT NULL;
ALTER TABLE qr_code MODIFY entity_type varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL;

Rename table
     payment_analytics to payment_analytics_tmp,
     new_payment_analytics to payment_analytics,
     payment_analytics_tmp to new_payment_analytics;

Drop table new_payment_analytics;

ALTER TABLE qr_payment ADD payer_bank_account_id char(14) DEFAULT NULL;

ALTER TABLE qr_code ADD request_source char(9) DEFAULT NULL;

ALTER TABLE addresses MODIFY COLUMN landmark VARCHAR(255) DEFAULT NULL;
